!module config:qinq.
!QinQ: Delete Qinq switch config-----------------------------------
!QinQ: Delete Qinq switch config-----------------------------------
!QinQ: Olt qinq domain config-----------------------------------
!---------------------------------------------------------------
!Basic command format:
!oltqinq-domain delete <name>
!oltqinq-domain modify <name> service-count <service-count>
!oltqinq-domain modify <name> service <1-8> type [single|share]
!oltqinq-domain <name> service <1-8> classification upstream {field-id <1-27> value <value> condition <condition>}*4 {serv-id <1-8>}*1
!oltqinq-domain <name> service <1-8> classification downstream {field-id <1-27> value <value> condition <condition>}*4
!oltqinq-domain <name> service <1-8> {vlan <1-4> user-vlanid [<0-4095>|null] user-cos [<0-7>|null] [add|translation|transparent] tpid <tpid> cos [<cos>|user-cos|null] vlanid [<vlanid>|null]}*4
!Key parameter interpretation:
!<1-8>: service index.
!<1-27>: 1: Destination MAC. 2: Source MAC. 3: Ethernet Type. 4: Fourth layer VLAN. 5: Third layer VLAN. 6: Second layer VLAN.
!        7: First layer VLAN. 8: TOS. 10: TTL. 11: Protocol type. 12: Source IPv4. 13: Source IPv6. 14: Destination IPv4.
!        15: Destination IPv6. 16: L4 source port. 17: L4 destination port. 18: Cos4. 19: Cos3. 20: Cos2. 21: Cos1. 22: Destination IPv6 prefix.
!        23: Source IPv6 prefix. 24: IP version. 25: IPv6 traffic class. 26: IPv6 flow label. 27: IPv6 next header.
!<condition>: 0: Never. 1: ==. 2: !=. 3: <=. 4: >=. 5: Exist. 6: No exist. 7: Always.
!---------------------------------------------------------------
!QinQ: Olt qinq domain config end-----------------------------------
